Compare confirmation bias lexicographic and in-group favoritism lexicographic revision.
We include these tests to see how group membership affects a biased agent.
First states and observables are created and then the plausibility orders of the agents.
The two agents have the same plausibility orders, but different stubbornness degrees. 

200 randomly created tests will be generated and the success percentage will be displayed in the end.
